 The troubles of the new civilization, the new civilization is not taking much privacy, it easily shows its thighs and jaws
 It has crushed many civilizations but it has been coped with very old things which people have yet believed that its fatigue can be understood as its aggression
 There are no alternatives to things such as stone fire or rain
 It is not to fail
 We should be submissive towards the ancestors
 More methods of living were known, as we have more knowledge of dying, between sticks and violent animal sounds, or taking birth on a straw in a riverbank meadow was not an archaic or uncivilized act, don't get your teeth raised and think about that justice too
 One who does not come to ask for the anniversary of democracy or as a reward for personal happiness, like the right of man, each one needs a little sky And it is necessary to have a land worth eating and sleeping, that people are innocent but they do not bear for many days Freedom is the oldest idea, what is the oldest wish, what can you teach us, while there is no room left to spit, you are new in your tricks, but you also have the sadness of a shopkeeper, with all the things you have surrounded us, a little more life than any of them
 It does not give except with some new medicines which are becoming rare every day and makes a vast world more helpless
 Don't laugh, it's a man's scream, not a machine, take him out of the machine
 Children are waiting for him at the house
 We want you to do something better with us, but know that you too have a lot of trouble that by this century you have invested a lot in things instead of men

 One does not have to wait for injustice
 If it happens one day, you will remember that it is happening every day, so many times you have not paid attention to it that it is done by someone else and you keep taking it as a simple news
 You keep looking at him and looking at him like an idol that it is happening on all sides, you think and drink tea that it is a matter of luck and you have someone in it If you do not think then you will also come to remember that you have done injustice unjustly, or that you have done injustice unjustly, not only that which you used to do by taking care of love, it was also injustice and what you did by turning away the blooming flower and then Even when you left your aspirations alone, and when you kept your right and your rights on things, look at the house itself, trees, water, sky, children, Woman and how many such things have been captured
 What greater injustice can be done than monopoly and look even in that so-called holy inner corner, which no one else can see, besides you there are still the signs of doing injustice

 'jaisha kaario olympicki mahila marathon main niraashajanak pradarshan rahaa

 jaisha ne kaha, 'vahaan kaaphi garmi thi

 hamaare liye naa hi pani kaa koi intjaam tha, na hi koi energy drink thi or na hi koi khaanaa

 sabhi deshon ke har do kimi par apane stall the, lekin hamaare desh kaa stall khaali tha

 jaisha ne kaha, 'hamen hamaare takneekee adhikariyon dwaara drink di jaani thi, yah niyam he

 ' a Delhi court has granted interim protection from the arrest of Shehla Rashid, a student leader of Jawaharlal Nehru University (JNU) and leader of the Jammu and Kashmir People's Movement
 bhartiya sena ke khilaaf kathith twit karne ke liye shehla par deshadroh kaa maamla darj kiya gaya he
 Giving interim protection to Rashid in the Patiala House Court, Additional Sessions Judge Pawan Kumar Jain said, "considering all the facts, i have come to the view that the case needs a detailed investigation
 tab tak aaropee ko giraftaar nahin kiya janaa chahie, haalanki jaanch adhikari (aaio) ke bulaane par unhen jaanch main shaamil hona hoga
 The court has fixed the next hearing of the case on November 5
 sunwaayee ke dauraan, atirikt jan abhiyojak ne kaha ki police ne shehla raashid ko abhi tak notice nahin diya he
 The accused's lawyer told the court that her client is ready to join the investigation and that she will cooperate with the police
 jan abhiyojak ne bhi kaha ki police ko abhi tak sena kii taraf se koi shikaayat nahin mili he
 He further said that the police needed at least six weeks to investigate the case
 police ne kaha ki jammu evam kashmir main maanavadhikaron ke kathith ulanghan ke sandarbh main shehla raashid ke bayanon ke aadhaar par unke khilaaf shuukravaar ko deshadroh kaa mukadmaa darj karaayaa gaya tha
 The special cell of Delhi Police said that a Sep 3 FIR was registered and a case of treason was registered on the criminal complaint of Supreme Court lawyer Alok Srivastava on Rashid, who had done his phd from JNU
 alok ne raashid kii giraftaar kii maang kii thi
 In a series of tweets, Rashid claimed that the Indian Army in the Valley was unrestrained, raising men, raiding homes and harassing people
 unhone daawa kiya tha ki kashmir main maanavadhikaron kaa ulanghan kiya ja rahaa he
 The Indian Army officially rejected these allegations and termed them baseless and unverified
 goa ke faib india showrooms main chipa camera lagane ke aarope main giraftaar 4 aropiyon ko shanivaar ko jamaanat mil gai
 24 hours later, these employees of Fab India, based in Candolim, Goa, were granted bail by the Magistrate Court on a personal bond of Rs 5000

 History of Pilibhit Talking about the parliamentary history of Pilibhit Lok Sabha seat, the Congress may have won from here in the Lok Sabha elections in 1951, but after that the Praja Socialist Party won the elections of 1957, 1962, 1967
 1971 main congress ko phir se yahaan par jeet mili, lekin 1977 main chali sarkaar virdohi lahar main congress kii karaari haar ho gai
 In the elections of 1980 and 1984, the Congress once again won big from here, but after that the Congress could never return here
 sanjay gandhi kii maut ke baad gandhi parivaar se alag hui menka gandhi ne 1989 main janata dal ke tikat par yahaan se chunaav ladaa or jeeta
 But two years later, in the 1991 elections, BJP started winning from here
 menka gandhi ne 1996 se 2004 tak lagaataar chaar baar yahaan se chunaav jeeta, inamen do baar nirdaleey or 2004 main bijepi ke tikat se chunaav main jeet hasil kii thi
 In 2009, he left this seat for his son Varun Gandhi and Varun was elected as an MP from here
 lekin 2014 main ek baar phir vah yahaan waapas ain or chhathin baar yahaan se saansad chuni gayi

 The Bhima app launched by Prime Minister Narendra Modi on 30 December has already become very popular and crores of people are using it
 aadhaar besd pement se judane ke baad mana ja rahaa he ki isamen din doguni raat chauguni pragati hogi
 Now the government is also giving cashback and bonus to download the Bhima app and refer it to others
 aaie ham aapako bataate hai un khaasiyaton ke bare main jisaki vajah se bhim sabhi i wolet, Paytm or debit credit card kaa baap sabit ho rahaa he :-1
 BHIM ie Bharat Interface For Money is run by the National Payments Corporation of India (NPCI), Government of India
 yani bharat sarkaar kaa ap hone kii vajah se aap is par puraa bharosa kar sakate hai
 The biggest feature of the Bhima app is its simplicity
 sirf 2 MB ke is ap ko kuch second ke bheetar hi Android yaa yphone main downlod kiya ja saktaa he
 This app has been designed in such a way that even the first time user can easily understand it
 bhim ap istemaal karne ke liye jaruri sirf yah he ki aapkaa bank acount aapke mobile number se judaa ho
 At present, Bhima App can be linked with only one bank account
 2
 After downloading the Bhima app from Google Play Store, for the first time to activate it, it is necessary that you have your debit card
 ap downlod karte hi aapako 4 disit kaa numberon vaala ek password bananaa padataa he
 After that some information has to be entered on the debit card
 bhim ap ko hindi angreji ke alaava tamambharatiya bhashaaon main istemaal kiya ja saktaa he
 Another password has to be created for money transactions
 yah password bhi chaar anko kaa hona chahie lekin yah ap kholane ke password se alag hona jaruri he
 That is, there are two passwords in the Bhima app for complete security
 pehla password bhim ap ko kholane ke liye or doosraa password paise kaa lenden karne ke liye
 That is, if you add the password created to lock the mobile phone, then there are three layers of security in the Bhima app
 pita chalaate hai kiraane kii dukaan, modi kii yojana se ban gai karodpati3
 You do not need to tell anyone your name, your bank, and even your bank account number to transact with the Bhima app
 paise kaa lenden 24 ghante main kabhi bhi or chuttee ke din bhi ho saktaa he
 Money transactions are absolutely free through the Bhima app
 4
 After activating the Bhima app, your UPI address becomes like an email
 aam taur par yah phone number @ upiai hota he jaise 9839098390@upi
 If you want, you can also change it to make UPI address of your choice
 kisi se bhim ap ke jariye lenden karne ke liye sirf yahi adress bataanaa jaruri he jo kiapake bank acount se judahota he
 If you want to send money to someone through the Bhima app and the other person has also activated the Bhima app, then you can verify it only after entering his phone number
 bhim ap ke bheetar phone number daalate hi us vyakti kaa naam aa jaae to iskaa matlab he ki usne bhim ap actevet kar rakhaa he
 5
 ab sarkaar ne bhim ke saath aadhaar ko bhi jod diya he
 That is, if a person has not started his Bhima app but his Aadhaar card is linked with his bank account, then you can send money to him by entering the Aadhaar number
 gas kii sabsidi bank acount se jude hone kii vajah se ab zyaadaatar logon ne apana aadhaar bank se judwa liya he
 6
 duusare i vallett se bhi is myne main alag he ki yahaan aapako kharch karne ke liye pehle se kisi velette main paise daalane kii jarurat nahin he
 While spending money, it directly goes out of your bank account and reaches another person's bank account
 Paytm jaise i vallett main jo paisa aap daalate hai us par aapako koi interest nahin miltaa
 But because the money from Bhima goes directly to your bank account, you also get interest on whatever money comes in your bank account
 7
 You can also create QR code through the Bhima app
 iskaa print out nikaal kar dukandaar apane dukaan par chipka sakate hai
 The person who has to pay can scan this QR code directly and pay immediately
 8
 Apart from sending money to someone through the Bhima app, you can also ask for money from someone
 maange gaye paise kii request us vyakti ke bhim ap par jaati he or agar vah vyakti apana passworddalakar use oke kar de to paisa fauranapke acount main aa saktaa he
 For example, if many friends meet and party together, then one person can make a payment there and ask the rest of the people to pay their share
 9
 Once someone is registered in Bhima, then payment can also be made without internet
 yahaan tak ki smartphone kii jarurat bhi nahin he
 For this, all options come automatically by dialing * 99 #

 agar uskaa aadhaar number apane bank acount se judaa hua he to graahak apana angootha lagaakar dukandaar ko pement kar saktaa he

 rajya main bhartiya janata party pichley 15 varshon se satta main he or is baar vah 65 siton par jeet ke saath chauthi baar sarkaar banane kii koshish kar rahi he
 At the same time, the Congress is trying to come to power this time
 kashmir main deshhit main banaaya gaya gathbandhan deshhit main tod diya gaya
 Country interest is the maida with which politics sometimes makes puri, sometimes samosa
 aaj isi deshhit ke tahat bijepi ne gathbandhan se alag hone kaa elaan kar diya
 The BJP and PDP continued to run the government together for three years
 aaj achaanak media main mahabuuba sarkaar bolaa jane laga he magar kya ham bhul gaye hai ki us sarkaar main bijepi ke das mantri the jinamein ek up mukhyamantri bhi the
 If the situation in Jammu and Kashmir has become so worrying, then its responsibility is only on Mehbooba Mufti or it is the responsibility of both BJP and PDP
 kashmir kii sarkaar jitani kashmir se chalati he utani hi dilli kii nitiyon se chalati he
 Has Delhi's policies failed there? How will Delhi accept accountability for the situation in Kashmir? If Kashmir's policy was to be carried out with guns, then its results are telling those who wanted to run with guns
 agar baatcheet se chalani thi use naakaam vahi bataa rahe hai jo bich bich main baatcheet ke naam par sizafire kar dete hai
 The work of these old photographs is now so much that the files on the channel will continue to run with the tag, but the sad aspect of Kashmir politics is that it does not progress beyond the old file
 ab aap taiyaar ho jaaiye ki sofe par baithe muskuraate ye netaa ab baahar aise bayaan denge jaise kabhi saath chaay bhi na pi ho
 The Kashmir debate is a complex debate but it is for the scholars
 akhabaaron ke sampadakeey pannon se baahar aam logon ke bich kashmir ko lekar ek do line jisamen garmjoshi bhare naare hi kaaphi hai
 The line that Delhi decides on Kashmir also accounts for what benefits it will get in Hindi speaking states
 tay karnaa mushkil he ki kashmir kaa faisla kashmir ke liye hota he yaa phir hindi bhashi pradeshon kii raajnneeti ko set karne ke liye hota he
 In February 2015, the BJP PDP government was formed, its strategist Ram Madhav was told in the media, the same Ram Madhav announced the end of this alliance on 19 June 2018
 is saal april main ram madhav ke kai bayaan chape mili jisamen ve saaf saaf kah rahe hai ki gathbandhan main koi khatas nahin he
 There is no danger
 vahi ram madhav do maheene baad bataa rahe hai ki gathbandhan chalane laayak nahin he
 After Mufti Sahab's death, Mehbooba Mufti took a long time to form an alliance, but she finally agreed
 kashmir main halaat bighad chuke hai yah sabko pataa he
 You will hear this from everyone's tongue
 bijepi ko bataanaa chahie ki jis gathbandhan ko wo aitihaasik avasar bataa rahi thi, uskaa itihaas teen saal hi kyon tikaa he
 On 1 March 2015, the Prime Minister's tweet was also brought out from the ruins of the same history where this coalition is now buried
 kashmir main rajyapal kaa shashan hoga
 The addition subtraction to be done by which party has the number is so much so that the screens of the channels are kept busy
 enen vohara kashmir chalaayenge
 Congress and NC have made it clear that they are not in this race
 na aapas main or na kisi or ke saath milakar sarkaar nahin banaaenge
 It is not right to say mismatched alliance, if it was mismatched, it would not have lasted for three years
 aisi baat nahin he ki is dauraan chunautiyaan nahin ain
 She was enough to break the alliance, but still the government continued
 tab bhi chali jab patharbazi charam par thi, halaat bekaabu ho chale the
 It used to run pictures on news channels day and night and opinion was made in Hindi states
 magar patharbazi ke drishy bataa rahe the ki halaat bekaabu hai
 The gap of mistrust is widening
 phir isi saal farvari 2018 main ek khabar chupake se aakar chali jaati he ki 2008 se 2017 ke bich 11,000 logon ke khilaaf patharbazi karne ke mukademe darj the, un sabase mukadmaa waapas liya jaataa he
 Thousands of people were arrested in the year 2016 when the stone pelting was at its peak
 isi 7 june 2018 ko grahamantri rajnath singh ne jammu kashmir sports kanklev main kaha tha ki bacchon ke khilaaf patharbazi karne ke jitne bhi cese kiye gaye the unhen waapas liya jayega
 This means that the Central and State Governments were proceeding thoughtfully together in the matter of withdrawing the case from the stone pelters
 yahi baat ram madhav bhi kah chuke hai
 You can also see an interview of Ram Madhav released from PTI on 30 April 2018 in which he says that for the first time the state government has given an apology by talking to the Home Ministry
 isi bich aapako yaad hoga ki ek major gogai seen main pravesh karte hai, apni jeep par ek faruk ahamed daar ko baandh kar dhaal bana lete hai
 The matter was also disputed and the bravery of the army and the strong intentions of the government were praised
 isi saal 23 may main major gogai ko ek hotel main kathith rup se naaballig ladki ke saath pakadaa jaataa he or inke khilaaf sena court aaf inquairi ke aadesh detii he
 From these two examples, you can see how the issues on which the political thinking of the Hindi territories was tried in a particular mold ends
 in tamaam chunautiyon ke bich ek chiz tiki rahi to wo pidipi bijepi kii sarkaar
 In the case of Kathua rape, this alliance remained intact, while two BJP ministers had to be removed at the behest of Mehbooba
 jo balaatkaar ke aaropee ke paksh main sabha kar rahe the
 If Mehbooba's bus would have gone on these two ministers, they would not have gone to the assembly in favor of the accused
 vahi mahabuuba chaahakar par shopiyaan maamle main major aditya kumaar kaa naam exiaar main nahin daal pain, jabaki ve twit kar magistrate jaanch ke aadesh de chuki thi
 Obviously both had to bend and both continued to walk together
 ram madhav ne bahut aasaani se mahabuuba ko gathbandhan kaa mukhya netritv qaraar de diya magar yah bhi bahes kaa mudda he ki mahabuuba ke haath main kitna netritv tha

 ve bas kathputlati rah gayi hai

 Kashmir is not an unknown place for the Prime Minister
 tippaniyan Read all his speeches given in Kashmir after 2014, i read four to five speeches
 unamem kashmir kii niti kaa koi sanket nahin miltaa he, bas vikaas kii bate hai

 puraa bhaashan yojanaon ke shilanyas udghaatan or unke phaayde ko lekar hota tha
